\DoxyCodeLine{1762 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1763                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} prev\_MaterialIndex = m\_currentMaterialIndex;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1764                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} isUsingAltTypeface = m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].isUsingAlternateTypeface;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1765 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1766                 m\_isParsingText = \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1767 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1768                 \textcolor{comment}{// When using Linked text, mark character as ignored and skip to next character.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1769                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_characterCount < m\_firstVisibleCharacter)}

\DoxyCodeLine{1771                     m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].isVisible = \textcolor{keyword}{false};}

\DoxyCodeLine{1773                     m\_characterCount += 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1774                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{continue};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1775                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1776 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1777                 \textcolor{comment}{// Handle Font Styles like LowerCase, UpperCase and SmallCaps.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1779 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1780                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} smallCapsMultiplier = 1.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1781 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1782                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_textElementType == TMP\_TextElementType.Character)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1783                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1784                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((m\_style \& FontStyles.UpperCase) == FontStyles.UpperCase)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1785                     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1786                         \textcolor{comment}{// If this character is lowercase, switch to uppercase.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1787                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}.IsLower((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char})charCode))}
\DoxyCodeLine{1788                             charCode = \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}.ToUpper((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char})charCode);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1789 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1790                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1791                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((m\_style \& FontStyles.LowerCase) == FontStyles.LowerCase)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1792                     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1793                         \textcolor{comment}{// If this character is uppercase, switch to lowercase.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1794                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}.IsUpper((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char})charCode))}
\DoxyCodeLine{1795                             charCode = \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}.ToLower((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char})charCode);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1796                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1797                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((m\_fontStyle \& FontStyles.SmallCaps) == FontStyles.SmallCaps || (m\_style \& FontStyles.SmallCaps) == FontStyles.SmallCaps)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1798                     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1799                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}.IsLower((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char})charCode))}
\DoxyCodeLine{1800                         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1801                             smallCapsMultiplier = 0.8f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1802                             charCode = \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}.ToUpper((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char})charCode);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1803                         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1804                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1805                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1806 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                \#endregion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1807 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1808 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1809                 \textcolor{comment}{// Look up Character Data from Dictionary and cache it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1810 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                \#region Look up Character Data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1811                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_textElementType == TMP\_TextElementType.Sprite)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1812                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1813                     \textcolor{comment}{// If a sprite is used as a fallback then get a reference to it and set the color to white.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1815                     m\_currentSpriteAsset = m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].spriteAsset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1816                     m\_spriteIndex = m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].spriteIndex;}

\DoxyCodeLine{1819                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (sprite == \textcolor{keyword}{null}) \textcolor{keywordflow}{continue};}

\DoxyCodeLine{1824                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1826 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1827                     \textcolor{comment}{// The sprite scale calculations are based on the font asset assigned to the text object.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1829                     currentElementScale = m\_currentFontAsset.\mbox{\hyperlink{classTMPro_1_1TMP__FontAsset_a6afd05863cb5c5f39221cc63904b3f90}{fontInfo}}.Ascender / sprite.height * sprite.scale * spriteScale;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1830 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1831                     m\_cached\_TextElement = sprite;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1832 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1833                     m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].elementType = TMP\_TextElementType.Sprite;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1834                     m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].scale = spriteScale;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1835                     m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].spriteAsset = m\_currentSpriteAsset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1836                     m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].fontAsset = m\_currentFontAsset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1837                     m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].materialReferenceIndex = m\_currentMaterialIndex;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1838 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1839                     m\_currentMaterialIndex = prev\_MaterialIndex;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1840 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1841                     padding = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1842                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1843                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_textElementType == TMP\_TextElementType.Character)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1844                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1845                     m\_cached\_TextElement = m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].textElement;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1846                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_cached\_TextElement == \textcolor{keyword}{null}) \textcolor{keywordflow}{continue};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1847 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1848                     m\_currentFontAsset = m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].fontAsset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1849                     m\_currentMaterial = m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].material;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1850                     m\_currentMaterialIndex = m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].materialReferenceIndex;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1851 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1852                     \textcolor{comment}{// Re-\/calculate font scale as the font asset may have changed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1853                     m\_fontScale = m\_currentFontSize * smallCapsMultiplier / m\_currentFontAsset.\mbox{\hyperlink{classTMPro_1_1TMP__FontAsset_a6afd05863cb5c5f39221cc63904b3f90}{fontInfo}}.PointSize * m\_currentFontAsset.\mbox{\hyperlink{classTMPro_1_1TMP__FontAsset_a6afd05863cb5c5f39221cc63904b3f90}{fontInfo}}.Scale * (m\_isOrthographic ? 1 : 0.1f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1854 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1856 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1857                     m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].elementType = TMP\_TextElementType.Character;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1858                     m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].scale = currentElementScale;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1859 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1860                     padding = m\_currentMaterialIndex == 0 ? m\_padding : m\_subTextObjects[m\_currentMaterialIndex].\mbox{\hyperlink{classTMPro_1_1TMP__SubMesh_adc8e38d6679306c54598bf48db166a3f}{padding}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1861                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1940                 \textcolor{comment}{// Set Padding based on selected font style}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1941 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                \#region Handle Style Padding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1942                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_textElementType == TMP\_TextElementType.Character \&\& !isUsingAltTypeface \&\& ((m\_style \& FontStyles.Bold) == FontStyles.Bold || (m\_fontStyle \& FontStyles.Bold) == FontStyles.Bold)) \textcolor{comment}{// Checks for any combination of Bold Style.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1943                 \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{1948 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1950                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (style\_padding + padding > gradientScale)}

\DoxyCodeLine{1954                         style\_padding = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1955 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1956                     bold\_xAdvance\_multiplier = 1 + m\_currentFontAsset.boldSpacing * 0.01f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1957                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1958                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1959                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1960                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_currentMaterial.HasProperty(ShaderUtilities.ID\_GradientScale))}
\DoxyCodeLine{1961                     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1962                         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} gradientScale = m\_currentMaterial.GetFloat(ShaderUtilities.ID\_GradientScale);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1963                         style\_padding = m\_currentFontAsset.normalStyle / 4.0f * gradientScale * m\_currentMaterial.GetFloat(ShaderUtilities.ID\_ScaleRatio\_A);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1964 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1965                         \textcolor{comment}{// Clamp overall padding to Gradient Scale size.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1966                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (style\_padding + padding > gradientScale)}

\DoxyCodeLine{1973                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1975 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1976 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1977                 \textcolor{comment}{// Determine the position of the vertices of the Character or Sprite.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1978 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                \#region Calculate Vertices Position}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1979                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} fontBaseLineOffset = m\_currentFontAsset.\mbox{\hyperlink{classTMPro_1_1TMP__FontAsset_a6afd05863cb5c5f39221cc63904b3f90}{fontInfo}}.Baseline * m\_fontScale * m\_fontScaleMultiplier * m\_currentFontAsset.\mbox{\hyperlink{classTMPro_1_1TMP__FontAsset_a6afd05863cb5c5f39221cc63904b3f90}{fontInfo}}.Scale;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1980                 Vector3 top\_left;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1981                 top\_left.x = m\_xAdvance + ((m\_cached\_TextElement.xOffset -\/ padding -\/ style\_padding + glyphAdjustments.xPlacement) * currentElementScale * (1 -\/ m\_charWidthAdjDelta));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1982                 top\_left.y = fontBaseLineOffset + (m\_cached\_TextElement.yOffset + padding + glyphAdjustments.yPlacement) * currentElementScale -\/ m\_lineOffset + m\_baselineOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1983                 top\_left.z = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1984 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1985                 Vector3 bottom\_left;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1986                 bottom\_left.x = top\_left.x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1987                 bottom\_left.y = top\_left.y -\/ ((m\_cached\_TextElement.height + padding * 2) * currentElementScale);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1988                 bottom\_left.z = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1989 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1990                 Vector3 top\_right;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1991                 top\_right.x = bottom\_left.x + ((m\_cached\_TextElement.width + padding * 2 + style\_padding * 2) * currentElementScale * (1 -\/ m\_charWidthAdjDelta));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1992                 top\_right.y = top\_left.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1993                 top\_right.z = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1994 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1995                 Vector3 bottom\_right;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1996                 bottom\_right.x = top\_right.x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1997                 bottom\_right.y = bottom\_left.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1998                 bottom\_right.z = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1999 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                \#endregion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2000 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2001 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2002                 \textcolor{comment}{// Check if we need to Shear the rectangles for Italic styles}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2003 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                \#region Handle Italic \& Shearing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2004                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_textElementType == TMP\_TextElementType.Character \&\& !isUsingAltTypeface \&\& ((m\_style \& FontStyles.Italic) == FontStyles.Italic || (m\_fontStyle \& FontStyles.Italic) == FontStyles.Italic))}
\DoxyCodeLine{2005                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2006                     \textcolor{comment}{// Shift Top vertices forward by half (Shear Value * height of character) and Bottom vertices back by same amount. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{2007                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} shear\_value = m\_currentFontAsset.italicStyle * 0.01f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2008                     Vector3 topShear = \textcolor{keyword}{new} Vector3(shear\_value * ((m\_cached\_TextElement.yOffset + padding + style\_padding) * currentElementScale), 0, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2009                     Vector3 bottomShear = \textcolor{keyword}{new} Vector3(shear\_value * (((m\_cached\_TextElement.yOffset -\/ m\_cached\_TextElement.height -\/ padding -\/ style\_padding)) * currentElementScale), 0, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2010 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2011                     top\_left = top\_left + topShear;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2012                     bottom\_left = bottom\_left + bottomShear;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2013                     top\_right = top\_right + topShear;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2014                     bottom\_right = bottom\_right + bottomShear;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2015                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2016 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                \#endregion Handle Italics \& Shearing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2017 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2018 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2019                 \textcolor{comment}{// Handle Character Rotation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2020 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                \#region Handle Character Rotation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2021                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_isFXMatrixSet)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2022                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2023                     \textcolor{comment}{// Apply scale matrix when simulating Condensed text.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2024                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_FXMatrix.m00 != 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2025                     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2026                         \textcolor{comment}{//top\_left = m\_FXMatrix.MultiplyPoint3x4(top\_left);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2027                         \textcolor{comment}{//bottom\_left = m\_FXMatrix.MultiplyPoint3x4(bottom\_left);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2028                         \textcolor{comment}{//top\_right = m\_FXMatrix.MultiplyPoint3x4(top\_right);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2029                         \textcolor{comment}{//bottom\_right = m\_FXMatrix.MultiplyPoint3x4(bottom\_right);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2030                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2031 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2032                     Vector3 positionOffset = (top\_right + bottom\_left) / 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2033 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2034                     top\_left = m\_FXMatrix.MultiplyPoint3x4(top\_left -\/ positionOffset) + positionOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2035                     bottom\_left = m\_FXMatrix.MultiplyPoint3x4(bottom\_left -\/ positionOffset) + positionOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2036                     top\_right = m\_FXMatrix.MultiplyPoint3x4(top\_right -\/ positionOffset) + positionOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2037                     bottom\_right = m\_FXMatrix.MultiplyPoint3x4(bottom\_right -\/ positionOffset) + positionOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2038                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2039 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                \#endregion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2040 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2041 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2042                 \textcolor{comment}{// Store vertex information for the character or sprite.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2043                 m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].bottomLeft = bottom\_left;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2044                 m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].topLeft = top\_left;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2045                 m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].topRight = top\_right;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2046                 m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].bottomRight = bottom\_right;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2047 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2048                 m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].origin = m\_xAdvance;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2049                 m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].baseLine = fontBaseLineOffset -\/ m\_lineOffset + m\_baselineOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2050                 m\_textInfo.characterInfo[m\_characterCount].aspectRatio = (top\_right.x -\/ bottom\_left.x) / (top\_left.y -\/ bottom\_left.y);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2051 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2052 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2053                 \textcolor{comment}{// Compute and save text element Ascender and maximum line Ascender.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2653                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (charCode == 9)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2654                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2655                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} tabSize = m\_currentFontAsset.\mbox{\hyperlink{classTMPro_1_1TMP__FontAsset_a6afd05863cb5c5f39221cc63904b3f90}{fontInfo}}.TabWidth * currentElementScale;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2656                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} tabs = Mathf.Ceil(m\_xAdvance / tabSize) * tabSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2657                     m\_xAdvance = tabs > m\_xAdvance ? tabs : m\_xAdvance + tabSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2658                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2659                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_monoSpacing != 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2660                 \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{2662 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2663                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}.IsWhiteSpace((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char})charCode) || charCode == 0x200B)}

\DoxyCodeLine{2665                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2666                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!m\_isRightToLeft)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2667                 \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{2670 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2671                     m\_xAdvance += ((m\_cached\_TextElement.xAdvance * scaleFXMultiplier * bold\_xAdvance\_multiplier + m\_characterSpacing + m\_currentFontAsset.normalSpacingOffset + glyphAdjustments.xAdvance) * currentElementScale + m\_cSpacing) * (1 -\/ m\_charWidthAdjDelta);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2672 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2675                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2676                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2677                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2678                     m\_xAdvance -\/= glyphAdjustments.xAdvance * currentElementScale;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2679                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3173                     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3174                         \textcolor{comment}{// CHARACTERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3175                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} TMP\_TextElementType.Character:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3176                             Extents lineExtents = lineInfo.lineExtents;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3177                             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} uvOffset = (m\_uvLineOffset * currentLine) \% 1; \textcolor{comment}{// + m\_uvOffset.x;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3178 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3179                             \textcolor{comment}{// Setup UV2 based on Character Mapping Options Selected}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3180 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                            \#region Handle UV Mapping Options}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3181                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (m\_horizontalMapping)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3182                             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3183                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} TextureMappingOptions.Character:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3184                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.x = 0; \textcolor{comment}{//+ m\_uvOffset.x;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3185                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.x = 0; \textcolor{comment}{//+ m\_uvOffset.x;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3186                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.x = 1; \textcolor{comment}{//+ m\_uvOffset.x;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3187                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.uv2.x = 1; \textcolor{comment}{//+ m\_uvOffset.x;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3188                                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3189 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3190                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} TextureMappingOptions.Line:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3191                                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_textAlignment != TextAlignmentOptions.Justified)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3192                                     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3193                                         characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.x = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.position.x -\/ lineExtents.min.x) / (lineExtents.max.x -\/ lineExtents.min.x) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3194                                         characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.x = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.position.x -\/ lineExtents.min.x) / (lineExtents.max.x -\/ lineExtents.min.x) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3195                                         characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.x = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.position.x -\/ lineExtents.min.x) / (lineExtents.max.x -\/ lineExtents.min.x) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3196                                         characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.uv2.x = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.position.x -\/ lineExtents.min.x) / (lineExtents.max.x -\/ lineExtents.min.x) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3197                                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3198                                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3199                                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{comment}{// Special Case if Justified is used in Line Mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3200                                     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3201                                         characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.x = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.position.x + justificationOffset.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) / (m\_meshExtents.max.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3202                                         characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.x = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.position.x + justificationOffset.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) / (m\_meshExtents.max.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3203                                         characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.x = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.position.x + justificationOffset.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) / (m\_meshExtents.max.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3204                                         characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.uv2.x = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.position.x + justificationOffset.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) / (m\_meshExtents.max.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3205                                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3206                                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3207 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3208                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} TextureMappingOptions.Paragraph:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3209                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.x = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.position.x + justificationOffset.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) / (m\_meshExtents.max.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3210                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.x = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.position.x + justificationOffset.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) / (m\_meshExtents.max.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3211                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.x = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.position.x + justificationOffset.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) / (m\_meshExtents.max.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3212                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.uv2.x = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.position.x + justificationOffset.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) / (m\_meshExtents.max.x -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.x) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3213                                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3214 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3215                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} TextureMappingOptions.MatchAspect:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3216 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3217                                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (m\_verticalMapping)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3218                                     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3219                                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} TextureMappingOptions.Character:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3220                                             characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y = 0; \textcolor{comment}{//+ m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3221                                             characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y = 1; \textcolor{comment}{//+ m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3222                                             characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.y = 0; \textcolor{comment}{//+ m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3223                                             characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.uv2.y = 1; \textcolor{comment}{//+ m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3224                                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3225 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3226                                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} TextureMappingOptions.Line:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3227                                             characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.position.y -\/ lineExtents.min.y) / (lineExtents.max.y -\/ lineExtents.min.y) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3228                                             characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.position.y -\/ lineExtents.min.y) / (lineExtents.max.y -\/ lineExtents.min.y) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3229                                             characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.y = characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3230                                             characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.uv2.y = characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3231                                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3232 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3233                                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} TextureMappingOptions.Paragraph:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3234                                             characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.position.y -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.y) / (m\_meshExtents.max.y -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.y) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3235                                             characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.position.y -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.y) / (m\_meshExtents.max.y -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.y) + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3236                                             characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.y = characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3237                                             characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.uv2.y = characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3238                                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3239 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3240                                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} TextureMappingOptions.MatchAspect:}

\DoxyCodeLine{3243                                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3244 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3245                                     \textcolor{comment}{//float xDelta = 1 -\/ (\_uv2s[vert\_index + 0].y * textMeshCharacterInfo[i].AspectRatio); // Left aligned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3246                                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} xDelta = (1 -\/ ((characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y + characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y) * characterInfos[i].aspectRatio)) / 2; \textcolor{comment}{// Center of Rectangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3247 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3248                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.x = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y * characterInfos[i].aspectRatio) + xDelta + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3249                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.x = characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3250                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.x = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y * characterInfos[i].aspectRatio) + xDelta + uvOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3251                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.uv2.x = characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3252                                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3253                             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3254 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3255                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (m\_verticalMapping)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3256                             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3257                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} TextureMappingOptions.Character:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3258                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y = 0; \textcolor{comment}{//+ m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3259                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y = 1; \textcolor{comment}{//+ m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3260                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.y = 1; \textcolor{comment}{//+ m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3261                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.uv2.y = 0; \textcolor{comment}{//+ m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3262                                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3263 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3264                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} TextureMappingOptions.Line:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3265                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.position.y -\/ lineInfo.descender) / (lineInfo.ascender -\/ lineInfo.descender); \textcolor{comment}{// + m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3266                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.position.y -\/ lineInfo.descender) / (lineInfo.ascender -\/ lineInfo.descender); \textcolor{comment}{// + m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3267                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.y = characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3268                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.uv2.y = characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3269                                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3270 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3271                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} TextureMappingOptions.Paragraph:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3272                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.position.y -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.y) / (m\_meshExtents.max.y -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.y); \textcolor{comment}{// + m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3273                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y = (characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.position.y -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.y) / (m\_meshExtents.max.y -\/ m\_meshExtents.min.y); \textcolor{comment}{// + m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3274                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.y = characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3275                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.uv2.y = characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3276                                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3277 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3278                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} TextureMappingOptions.MatchAspect:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3279                                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} yDelta = (1 -\/ ((characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.x + characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.x) / characterInfos[i].aspectRatio)) / 2; \textcolor{comment}{// Center of Rectangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3280 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3281                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y = yDelta + (characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.x / characterInfos[i].aspectRatio); \textcolor{comment}{// + m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3282                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y = yDelta + (characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.x / characterInfos[i].aspectRatio); \textcolor{comment}{// + m\_uvOffset.y;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3283                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_BR.uv2.y = characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3284                                     characterInfos[i].vertex\_TR.uv2.y = characterInfos[i].vertex\_TL.uv2.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3285                                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3286                             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3287 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                            \#endregion}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3302                             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} y0 = characterInfos[i].vertex\_BL.uv2.y;}
